;
; Initializes the stack
;
3471 D1            InitStack:   pop de                      ; DE := return address to the pager
3472 E1                         pop hl                      ; HL := return value to the caller
3473 ED 7B B2 5C                ld sp,($5CB2)               ; SP := RAMTOP
3477 06 3E                      ld b,$3E                    ; Put the $3E marker (end of the stack) to the stack
3479 C5                         push bc                     
347A ED 73 0B 5C                ld ($5C0B),sp               ; Store SP to DEFADD
347E E5                         push hl                     ; Restore caller return address
347F ED 73 3D 5C                ld ($5C3D),sp               ; Store SP to ERR-SP
3483 D5                         push de                     ; Restore return address to the pager
3484 C9                         ret                         ; Done
;
;
;
